**1)** — *apa* sich vergehen: *yo yasteṣāmapacarettamācakṣīta vai dvijaḥ*
[MBH. 12,9566.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.9566) *pitṛdevarṣibhṛtyāśca na cāpacaritā mayā*
[MĀRK. P. 13,13.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/markandeyapurana/app1?13,13)

- **RU:** — *apa* погрешать, проступиться: *yo yasteṣāmapacarettamācakṣīta vai dvijaḥ*
[MBH. 12,9566.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.9566) *pitṛdevarṣibhṛtyāśca na cāpacaritā mayā*
[MĀRK. P. 13,13.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/markandeyapurana/app1?13,13)
- **EN:** *apa* to transgress, do wrong: *yo yasteṣāmapacarettamācakṣīta vai dvijaḥ*
[MBH. 12,9566.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?12.9566) *pitṛdevarṣibhṛtyāśca na cāpacaritā mayā*
[MĀRK. P. 13,13.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/markandeyapurana/app1?13,13)
  <sub>attested</sub>

- **EN:** Vgl. *apacarita, apacāra* fg.

[102.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?9,102) *yathaivāhaṃ nābhicare kadācitpatīnmadādvai manasāpi jātu*
[MBH. 4,457.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?4.457)

## vyabhicar

`car~~h0_12_vya_bi`


**1)** — *vyabhi*
 1) sich feindselig gegen Jmd (acc. gen.) benehmen, sich vergehen:

*abrāhmaṇaṃ kartumicchanti raudrāste māṃ yathā vyabhicaranti nityam*
[MBH. 1,3234.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.3234) *na brahmadattaste bhūyo vyabhicariṣyati*
[KATHĀS. 20,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,4) [2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,2) *bhartāramapi jīvantamanyānvyabhicarantyuta (nāryaḥ)*
[MBH. 3,12869.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.12869)

- **RU:** — *vyabhi*
 1) вести себя враждебно по отношению к кому-л. (acc. gen.), погрешать:

*abrāhmaṇaṃ kartumicchanti raudrāste māṃ yathā vyabhicaranti nityam*
[MBH. 1,3234.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.3234) *na brahmadattaste bhūyo vyabhicariṣyati*
[KATHĀS. 20,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,4) [2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,2) *bhartāramapi jīvantamanyānvyabhicarantyuta (nāryaḥ)*
[MBH. 3,12869.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.12869)
- **EN:** — *vyabhi* 1) to behave hostilely toward someone (acc. gen.), to transgress: *abrāhmaṇaṃ kartumicchanti raudrāste māṃ yathā vyabhicaranti nityam* [MBH. 1,3234.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?1.3234) *na brahmadattaste bhūyo vyabhicariṣyati* [KATHĀS. 20,4.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,4) [2.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/kss/index.html?20,2) *bhartāramapi jīvantamanyānvyabhicarantyuta (nāryaḥ)* [MBH. 3,12869.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/mbhcalc?3.12869)

[LĀṬY. 2,1,11.]

[LĀṬY. 2,1,11.]

[BHĀG. P. 4,18,5.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?4,18,5) *na vyabhicarati tavekṣā yayā hyabhihito bhāgavato dharmaḥ*
[6,16,43.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?6,16,43)

[1,16,5.] *kaṣāyaṃ kāle 'vacāritam* rechtzeitig angewandt
[2,415,13. 367,5. 381,6.]

[1,16,5.] *kaṣāyaṃ kāle 'vacāritam* применённый своевременно

## car

`car~~h0_15_a_byava`


**1)** — *abhyava* andringen, eindringen: *netpurastānnāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsyabhyavacarān*

- **RU:** — *abhyava* вторгаться, проникать: *netpurastānnāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsyabhyavacarān*
- **EN:** *abhyava* to press forward, to penetrate: *netpurastānnāṣṭrā rakṣāṃsyabhyavacarān*

[R. 2,39,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/ramayanaschl/?2,39,19)

**7)** — 7) verzehren (vgl. simpl. u. 5 am Ende): *pipīlikābhirācīrṇamedastvaṅmāṃsaśoṇitam*
[BHĀG. P. 7,13,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?7,13,15)
- **EN:** — 7) to consume (vgl. simpl. u. 5, at the end): *pipīlikābhirācīrṇamedastvaṅmāṃsaśoṇitam*
[BHĀG. P. 7,13,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?7,13,15)

**8)** — 8) *hastenācarati*
[KĀTY. ŚR. 3,6,9.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?3,6,9) [16,4,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?16,4,15) [16](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?16,4,16) erklärt der Schol. durch *agnau prareyati, prakṣipati* hineinwerfen; es wird wohl heissen mit der Hand herbeikommen d. i. nachhelfen, hineinschieben.
[SĀY.] zu [AIT. BR.] erklärt übrigens *caraṇa* auch durch *āhutiprakṣepa* . Es scheint ein technischer Ausdruck für eine best. Geberde zu sein.
- **EN:** — 8) *hastenācarati*
[KĀTY. ŚR. 3,6,9.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?3,6,9) [16,4,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?16,4,15) [16](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/katyasr/app1?16,4,16) the Schol. explains through *agnau prareyati, prakṣipati* to throw in; it presumably means to come up with the hand d. i. to help along, to push in.
[SĀY.] on [AIT. BR.] moreover explains *caraṇa* also through *āhutiprakṣepa*. It appears to be a technical term for a best. gesture.

**9)** — 9) *ācarita* herkömmlich, gebräuchlich (vgl. 6.): *ācaritaṃ tu notkramet* was herkömmlich —, Regel ist
[ṚV. PRĀT. 11,32.]
[ŚĀK. 108,22](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shakuntala/app2?108,22), v. l. _n._ ein herkömmliches Zwangsmittel
[M. 8,49.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,49) *dāraputrapaśūnhatvā* (wohl *hṛtvā* zu lesen;
v. l. *baddhvā) kṛtvā dvāropaveśanam . yatrārthī dāpyate 'rthaṃ svaṃ tadācaritamucyate ..*
[BṚHASP.] bei [KULL.] zu d. St. — Statt der falschen und keinen Sinn gebenden Causalform *ācarayet*
[PAÑCAT. IV,24](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app1?4,24) ist *āvarayet* zu lesen.
- **EN:** — 9) *ācarita* customary, usual (vgl. 6.): *ācaritaṃ tu notkramet* what is customary, the rule
[ṚV. PRĀT. 11,32.]
[ŚĀK. 108,22](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/shakuntala/app2?108,22), v. l. _n._ a customary means of compulsion
[M. 8,49.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/manu/index.html?8,49) *dāraputrapaśūnhatvā* (presumably to be read *hṛtvā*;
v. l. *baddhvā) kṛtvā dvāropaveśanam . yatrārthī dāpyate 'rthaṃ svaṃ tadācaritamucyate ..*
[BṚHASP.] in [KULL.] on d. St. — Instead of the false and meaningless causal form *ācarayet*
[PAÑCAT. IV,24](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/pantankose/app1?4,24), *āvarayet* is to be read.

**note)** — Vgl. *ācaraṇa* fgg., *ācāra, ācārya* .
- **EN:** — Vgl. *ācaraṇa* fgg., *ācāra, ācārya*.

**5)** — 5) pass. uneigentlich —, metaphorisch gebraucht sein, — zugeschrieben werden: *kālo 'yaṃ dviparārdhyākhyo nimeṣa* (loc.) *upacaryate . avyākṛtasyānantasya anāderjagadātmanaḥ ..*
[BHĀG. P. 3,11,37.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?3,11,37) *yathā loke svaśaktiṣu yodheṣu vartamānau jayaparājayau rājñi upacaryete* wie Sieg und Niederlage in der Welt uneigentlich dem Könige zugeschreiben werden, indem dieselben eigentlich seine Kämpfer treffen,
Sch. zu [SĀṂKHYAK. 21 (S. 78). 62 (S. 177).] *vibhaktā bhrātara ityatra ca dhanasya yadvibhaktitvaṃ tadbhrātṛṣūpacaryate*
[MALLIN.] zu [KIR. 1,1.] [SĀH. D. 8,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?8,7) [30,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?30,19) Hierher gehört wohl auch die Stelle: *tenopacaryate rāhuḥ . yāmyottarā śaśigatirgaṇite 'pyupacaryate tena*
[VARĀH. BṚH. S. 5,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?5,15)

- **RU:** — 5) pass. употребляться в переносном —, метафорическом смысле, — приписываться: *kālo 'yaṃ dviparārdhyākhyo nimeṣa* (loc.) *upacaryate . avyākṛtasyānantasya anāderjagadātmanaḥ ..*
[BHĀG. P. 3,11,37.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?3,11,37) *yathā loke svaśaktiṣu yodheṣu vartamānau jayaparājayau rājñi upacaryete* как победа и поражение в мире в переносном смысле приписываются царю, тогда как они в собственном смысле постигают его воинов,
Sch. к [SĀṂKHYAK. 21 (S. 78). 62 (S. 177).] *vibhaktā bhrātara ityatra ca dhanasya yadvibhaktitvaṃ tadbhrātṛṣūpacaryate*
[MALLIN.] к [KIR. 1,1.] [SĀH. D. 8,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?8,7) [30,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?30,19) Сюда относится, вероятно, также это место: *tenopacaryate rāhuḥ . yāmyottarā śaśigatirgaṇite 'pyupacaryate tena*
[VARĀH. BṚH. S. 5,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?5,15)
- **EN:** — 5) pass. to be used non-literally —, used metaphorically —, to be ascribed: *kālo 'yaṃ dviparārdhyākhyo nimeṣa* (loc.) *upacaryate . avyākṛtasyānantasya anāderjagadātmanaḥ ..*
[BHĀG. P. 3,11,37.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bhagp_bur/app1/?3,11,37) *yathā loke svaśaktiṣu yodheṣu vartamānau jayaparājayau rājñi upacaryete* just as victory and defeat in the world are non-literally ascribed to the king, since they actually befall his warriors,
Sch. to [SĀṂKHYAK. 21 (S. 78). 62 (S. 177).] *vibhaktā bhrātara ityatra ca dhanasya yadvibhaktitvaṃ tadbhrātṛṣūpacaryate*
[MALLIN.] to [KIR. 1,1.] [SĀH. D. 8,7.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?8,7) [30,19.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/sahityadarpana/app1?30,19) Here probably also belongs the passage: *tenopacaryate rāhuḥ . yāmyottarā śaśigatirgaṇite 'pyupacaryate tena*
[VARĀH. BṚH. S. 5,15.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/brihatsam/app1?5,15)
  <sub>attested</sub>

**etym)** — Vgl. *upacara* fg., *upacarya, upacāra* fg., *upacārya* .

- **RU:** — Vgl. *upacara* fg., *upacarya, upacāra* fg., *upacārya* .
- **EN:** — Vgl. *upacara* fg., *upacarya, upacāra* fg., *upacārya* .
  <sub>attested</sub>

## abhyudā+car

`car~~h1_10_a_byud_a`


**1)** — *abhyudā* caus.: *asuraviśaṃ ha vai devānabhyudācārya āsīt* [AIT. BR. 6,36.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?6,36) nach [SĀY.] *devānabhilakṣya ullaṅghanarūpamācaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tiraskṛtya āsīt* er machte sie die Götter überspringen d. h. verfehlen; eher wohl das Volk der Asura war herangezogen (lag im Felde; also *abhyudācarya* zu vermuthen) gegen die Götter. Uebrigens fällt die Vernachlässigung des Saṃdhi auf; vgl. auch [Ind. St. 9,307.]

- **RU:** — *abhyudā* caus.: *asuraviśaṃ ha vai devānabhyudācārya āsīt* [AIT. BR. 6,36.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?6,36) согласно [SĀY.] *devānabhilakṣya ullaṅghanarūpamācaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tiraskṛtya āsīt* он заставил их перескочить через богов d. h. уклониться; скорее же народ Asura приблизился (стоял в поле; итак, следует предполагать *abhyudācarya*) против богов. Примечательно также пренебрежение Saṃdhi; vgl. также [Ind. St. 9,307.]
- **EN:** — *abhyudā* caus.: *asuraviśaṃ ha vai devānabhyudācārya āsīt*
[AIT. BR. 6,36.](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/aitbr/app1?6,36) according to [SĀY.] *devānabhilakṣya ullaṅghanarūpamācaraṇaṃ kṛtvā tiraskṛtya āsīt* "he made them overleap the gods" d. h. "to miss"; rather probably "the people of Asura had advanced (lay in the field"; thus *abhyudācarya* is to be conjectured) "against the gods." Moreover the neglect of Saṃdhi is striking; vgl. also
[Ind. St. 9,307.]
  <sub>attested</sub>

## car

`car~~h0_zz_pw00`


**pw00-act)** √*car*, *carati* (selten Med.), Partic. *carita* und *cīrṇa*.
- **EN:** *car*, *carati* (rarely Med.), Partic. *carita* and *cīrṇa*.

**pw00-1)** — 1〉 sich regen, — bewegen, umherstreichen, fahren, wandern, sich verbreiten (von Belebtem und Unbelebtem).
- **EN:** — 1) to stir, — move, roam about, travel, wander, spread (of animate and inanimate things).

**pw00-2)** — 2〉 durchwandern, durchstreichen, durchlaufen; mit Acc.
- **EN:** — 2) to wander through, roam through, traverse; with Acc.

**pw00-3)** — 3〉 entlang-, nachgehen; mit Acc. [85,2](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?85).
- **EN:** — 3) to go along, follow after; with Acc. [85,2](https://sanskrit-lexicon-scans.github.io/bchrest2/index.html?85).

**pw00-4)** — 4〉 sich aufführen, — verhalten, — benehmen, verfahren, handeln, verfahren mit Jmd (Instr. oder Loc.).
- **EN:** — 4) to conduct oneself, — behave, — comport oneself, proceed, act, deal with someone (Instr. or Loc.).

## car

`car~~h0_zz_pwkvn`


**1)** *car* mit *anupari* in *˚cāram*.
- **EN:** *car* with *anupari* in *˚cāram*.

**2)** *car* mit *anvabhyava* heranschleichen [MAITR. S. 1,10,20 (160,17)].
- **EN:** *car* with *anvabhyava* to creep up to, sneak toward [MAITR. S. 1,10,20 (160,17)].

**3)** *car* mit *saha* gehen mit, so v. a. übereinstimmen mit, ähnlich sein [BĀLAR. 130,19]. — Mit *anvabhyava* 5. — Mit *upa* II. **˚upacarita* angenehm berührt —, sich angezogen fühlend durch [MAHĀVY. 10,29]. — Mit *pari* II. *˚cīrṇa* fein bedient [DIVYĀVAD. 421,20]. — Caus. = Simpl. mit *pari* 2〉 [MAHĀVY. 245,943]. [DIVYĀVAD. 1,6]. — Mit *anupari* 2.
